## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the fundamental ODE formulation in population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying environmental parameters.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, density-independent)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth, common in tumor/population models)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P + c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (reduced growth at low density without extinction threshold)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible asymmetric growth curve)
- Logistic with harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth with proportional harvesting)
- Logistic with constant harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth with constant removal)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (logistic with periodic environmental forcing)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P * c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (exponentially changing carrying capacity)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Power-law density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (generalized density-dependent growth)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (growth with density-dependent birth rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) reducing growth at high population
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → additional multiplicative factor (P*c - 1) or (P + c) creating non-monotonic per-capita growth
- Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing → multiplicative modulation by sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) on growth rate parameter
- Metabolic scaling in growth → difference of power laws: c0*P**c1 - c2*P**c3 (anabolism vs catabolism scaling differently with size)
- Carrying capacity as emergent ratio → equilibrium population at P* = growth_rate / competition_coefficient, so quadratic terms P² indicate intraspecific competition
- Logarithmic density dependence → log(c/P) terms indicate Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically
- Harvesting or immigration → additive constants or linear terms independent of the P*(1-cP) structure represent external population flux
- Time-dependent exponential environment → exp(c*t) multiplying carrying capacity or growth rate models deteriorating or improving habitat
